 			var setREVStartSize=function(){
 				try{var e=new Object,i=jQuery(window).width(),t=9999,r=0,n=0,l=0,f=0,s=0,h=0;
 					e.c = jQuery('#rev_slider_1_1');

 					errorMessage = "<span style='font-size:16px;color:#BC0C06;'>" + errorMessage + "</span>";
 						jQuery(sliderID).show().html(errorMessage);

             <!-- Custom Slider -->
             <script type="text/javascript">
              jQuery(document).ready(function($) {								
 						
 							var slider_el = $("#custom_slides_3742");
 							var active_class = " active ";
 							// Create Custom Icons Nav
 							slider_el.on("initialized.owl.carousel", function(e) {
 							
 			slider_el.prepend("<div class=\"section\"><div class=\"cs_nav\"></div></div>");						
 								
 								slider_el.find(".custom_slide_item").each( function(i, el) {
 									if(!$(this).parent(".owl-item").hasClass("cloned")){
 										var icon = $(this).data("icon");
 										var has_text = $(this).data("has_text");
 										var txt = $(this).data("txt");
 										var sub_txt = $(this).data("sub_txt");
 										var nav_item_class = (has_text!="") ? "has_text" : "has_no_text";
 										
 										if(i==0){
 											nav_item_class += active_class;
 										}
 										var icon_btn_html = "<div class=\"col span_1_of_6 cs_nav_item "+ nav_item_class +"\"><div class=\"cs_nav_icon\"><i class=\"" + icon + "\"></i></div>";
 										
 										if(has_text!="") {
 											icon_btn_html += "<div class=\"cs_sub_txt\">" + sub_txt + "</div><h4 class=\"cs_txt\">" + txt + "</h4>";
 										}
 										
 										icon_btn_html += "</div>";
 										
 										slider_el.find(".section .cs_nav").append(icon_btn_html);
 									}
 								});
 							});
 
 							slider_el.owlCarousel({
 									items: 				1,
 									autoHeight: 		true,
 									smartSpeed:			1000,
 									dots:				true,
 									slideBy: 			1,
 									navRewind: 			false,
 									rtl: 				false,
 									 mouseDrag:			false,	
 									
 									animateOut:"fadeOut",	animateIn: "fadeIn"
 							});
 
 							// Attach events to Custom Icons Nav
 							slider_el.find(".cs_nav_item").each( function(i, el) {
 								$(this).click(function(){
 									slider_el.find(".cs_nav_item").removeClass(active_class);
 									$(this).addClass(active_class);
 									slider_el.trigger("to.owl.carousel", i);
 								});
 							});
 							
 							// Call back to set Active Icon Nav TODO - bug when loop
 							slider_el.on("changed.owl.carousel",function(e) {
 								slider_el.find(".cs_nav_item").each( function(i, el) {
 									//console.log(e.item.index);
 									if(i == e.item.index) {
 										slider_el.find(".cs_nav_item").removeClass(active_class);
 										$(this).addClass(active_class);
 									}
 								});
 							});
 							
 						});
             </script>
             <style>
              #custom_slides_3742.owl-carousel .animated {
 							-webkit-animation-duration: 1000ms;
 							animation-duration: 1000ms;
 						}
             </style>
             <!-- Custom Slider :: END -->

                MercyGate church is a multi-cultural, multi-generational Church where people of all backgrounds and walks of life come together to worship, grow and discover authentic relationships. We are contemporary, upbeat and fun; but most importantly we are Christ-centered in all we do. Our vision as a church is to be a place where lives are changed, relationships restored and destinies are discovered. We look forward to having you as our guest soon and we are saving a seat for you and your family!    -Pastors Don and Jonna Gibson

                </span>

               <div class="accordion_content">
                <div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix">
                 <p>
                  Our services are casual and welcoming. You can wear a suit and tie but most people; including our Lead Pastor, will be in jeans. Our services are energetic and include practical teaching as well as an opportunity for you to receive or get prayer. There are classes for nursery age from zero to 5 years old and then kids classes for 6 to 11 years old. We have a coffee shop that includes soft drinks and pastries so if you skipped breakfast we can hook you up! Our Pastors speak the Word in way that you can apply it to you life and find freedom. You will not leave the same! We can’t wait for you to join us! Sunday 8:30am or 10:45am and Wednesday 7:00pm.
                 </p>
                </div>

                </p>

                 Where are you located?
                </span>
               </h4>
               <div class="accordion_content">
                Our actual physical address is: 9627 Eagle Drive Mont Belvieu, TX 77523. We are located off of I10 East exit #800 just outside of Baytown. Your GPS should find us!
                <p>
                 From Houston, Baytown area: Head on Interstate 10 East and exit #800 taking the curve to the right to get on Eagle Drive. You then drive over the highway and you will see us right off the highway on the left side of Eagle Drive.
                </p>
                <p>
                 From Beaumont: Take Interstate 10 West and Exit #800 and make a right and you will be on Eagle Drive. Continue through the light and we are on the left!
                </p>

               <div class="accordion_content">
                <div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix">
                 <p>
                  We LOVE children! We have a full nursery staff each week for both services on Sunday for under 5 and of course we have Kid’s classes for 5-11. Our main priority in the MercyGate nursery is to show them God’s love while teaching them His word. You can drop your children off with ease by checking them in at the entrance in front of the children’s wing or at the church entrance closest to Eagle drive.
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  Be prepared to show your ID the first time. Keeping your little ones safe and secure is a top priority for us. Each service you will receive an ID sticker that you must show when picking up your child. Keeping them safe, secure, and happy while you take time to receive what you need in service is what we love to do! We can’t wait to see you here!
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  At MercyGate Church we also have our own MercyGate Learning Center that operates 5 days a week and is a “Children’s Day Out”, “Day Care”, “After School Program” and a “Private Kindergarten”! For more information about these programs you can look at their website:

If you choose to park further away from the church; we have several golf carts ready and waiting for assist you.
                <p>
                 We have several entrances but the main one is the covered portico and it is the closest one to the coffee shop!
                </p>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="boc_spacing " style="height: 20px">
             </div>
             <div class="boc_spacing " style="height: 20px">
             </div>
             <div class="boc_spacing " style="height: 20px">
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="no_side_padding_in_responsive_column wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-4">
           <div class="vc_column-inner vc_custom_1426444523973">
            <div class="wpb_wrapper">
             <div class="acc_holder ">
              <div class="acc_item">
               <h4 class="accordion">
                <span class="acc_control ">
                </span>
                <span class="acc_heading">
                 Is there a dress code?
                </span>
               </h4>
               <div class="accordion_content">
                There is no dress code at Mercy Gate Church. Just come as you are, ready to recieve God’s Word and what He has for you.
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="acc_item">
               <h4 class="accordion">
                <span class="acc_control ">
                </span>
                <span class="acc_heading">
                 Service is early...do you have coffee?
                </span>
               </h4>
               <div class="accordion_content">
                From the moment you walk in the door you will smell coffee….good coffee. Why? Well we are all better people with coffee and we also have an actual coffee shop with custom espresso drinks, iced drinks as well as tea and sodas. There is also muffins and pastries for you to eat as well if you haven’t had breakfast yet. Come and hang out with us!
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="acc_item">
               <h4 class="accordion">
                <span class="acc_control ">
                </span>
                <span class="acc_heading">
                 When are your regular service times?
                </span>
               </h4>
               <div class="accordion_content">
                Sunday: 8:30am and 10:45am
                <br/>
                Wednesdays: 7pm we have our Adult bible study as well as MercyGate Youth &amp; MercyGate Kids  &amp; nursery Classes.
                <p>
                 *Kids &amp; Nursery classes are available at every regularly scheduled service
                </p>
                <p>
                 Home groups are as announced as well as Women &amp; Men events and bible studies. Check our our EVENTS Page for more info:
                 <a href="http://mercygatechurch.com/events/">
                  MercyGate Events
                 </a>
                </p>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="acc_item">
               <h4 class="accordion">
                <span class="acc_control ">
                </span>
                <span class="acc_heading">
                 What do you believe?
                </span>
               </h4>
               <div class="accordion_content">
                We believe that as a church we are to be a light to our community. We are a place where the hurting and hopeless come to get answers and leave with healing and hope. We believe that with the same measure of forgiveness that we have been given; that we also need to give out to others. We are the living, breathing hands and feet of Jesus. We aren’t just a club of believers that look cute but we are people on a mission to make a difference in this life. We are a family with ups and downs and issues; so do not be afraid to join us….none of us are perfect on this side of heaven!
                <p>
                 For a detailed list of our doctrinal beliefs you can check out this link:
                 <a href="https://ag.org/Beliefs/Statement-of-Fundamental-Truths">
                  Assemblies of God Fundamentals of Truth
                 </a>
                </p>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="boc_spacing " style="height: 20px">
             </div>
             <div class="boc_spacing " style="height: 20px">
             </div>
             <div class="boc_spacing " style="height: 20px">
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="no_side_padding_in_responsive_column wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-4">
           <div class="vc_column-inner vc_custom_1460172824859">
            <div class="wpb_wrapper">
             <div class="acc_holder ">
              <div class="acc_item">
               <h4 class="accordion">
                <span class="acc_control ">
                </span>
                <span class="acc_heading">
                 What if I have more questions?
                </span>
               </h4>
               <div class="accordion_content">
                If you have any questions you are more than welcome to fill out a “contact us” form on this website and a staff member will get with you as soon as they can. You can also call our church office which is open Monday-Thursday 8:30-4:30pm at 281-576-5201. We are happy to help!
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="acc_item">
               <h4 class="accordion">
                <span class="acc_control ">
                </span>
                <span class="acc_heading">
                 How do I get involved further?
                </span>
               </h4>
               <div class="accordion_content">
                We are so glad that you asked! We have a class called MercyGate 101 that is held every other month and is an ideal time to hear our Pastors vision and meet our staff. There will be a time to ask questions, sign up to volunteer and even become a member if you would like. We will also share ways that you connect via social media and sign up for some small groups, to volunteer and get involved with our outreaches! Remember that we give our 1st, 2nd and 3rd guest a gift so please visit the Connection Center to get yours!
                <p>
                 Check out our EVENTS Page by clicking here to see the next MercyGate 101 Class OR email us at info@mercygatechurch.com!
                 <a href="http://mercygatechurch.com/events/">
                  MercyGate Events
                 </a>

              <div class="acc_item">
               <h4 class="accordion">
                <span class="acc_control ">
                </span>
                <span class="acc_heading">
                 How do I find out about events at MGC?
                </span>
               </h4>
               <div class="accordion_content">
                GREAT Question! We have an EVENTS page here on this website and you can click here to get all the information you need! We hope you get involved with our family by joining us!
                <a href="http://mercygatechurch.com/events/">
                 MercyGate Events
                </a>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="acc_item">
               <h4 class="accordion">
                <span class="acc_control ">
                </span>
                <span class="acc_heading">
                 How do I learn more about how to be saved?
                </span>
               </h4>
               <div class="accordion_content">
                The Bible clearly teaches that Salvation is a gift from God (Ephesians 2:8). It is not brought about by anything that we do. Webster defines the term gift as “something voluntarily transferred by one person to another without compensation”. God’s plan of salvation is freely given without us doing anything more than accepting it.
                <p>
                 <em>
                  Here are a few simple steps to help us understand God’s plan
                 </em>
                 .
                </p>
                <p>
                 1. Acknowledge your sin and its end result.
                 <br/>
                 For all have sinned. Romans 3:23a
                 <br/>
                 For the wages of sin is death. Romans 6:23a
                </p>
                <p>
                 2. Believe that Jesus died for your sin.
                 <br/>
                 The gift of God is eternal life through Jesus Christ our Lord. Romans 6:23b
                </p>
                <p>
                 3. Confess your sin and ask him to save you.
                 <br/>
                 For whosoever shall call upon the name of the Lord shall be saved. Romans 10:13
                 <br/>
                 If we confess our sins, he is faithful and just to forgive us our sins, and to cleanse us from all unrighteousness. 1John 1:9
                </p>
                <p>
                 Also ask Him to help you make a commitment to live your life so that it pleases Him by a condition of repentance. Webster defines it as : “to turn from sin and dedicate oneself to the correction of one’s life”
                </p>
                <p>
                 Therefore if any man be in Christ, he is a new creature: old things are passed away; behold, all things are become new. 2Corinthians 5:17
                </p>
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  Dear Lord Jesus,
                 </strong>
                </p>
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  Thank You for dying on the cross for my sin. Please forgive me. Come into my life. I receive You as my Lord and Savior. Now, help me to live for You the rest of this life.
                 </strong>
                </p>
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  In the name of Jesus, I pray.
                 </strong>
                </p>
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  Amen.
                 </strong>
                </p>
                <p>
                 Some Christians call this type of prayer the Sinner’s Prayer. While there is no example of a sinner’s prayer in the Bible, it is based on Romans 10:9-10:
                </p>
                <p>
                 If you declare with your mouth, “Jesus is Lord,” and believe in your heart that God raised him from the dead, you will be saved. For it is with your heart that you believe and are justified, and it is with your mouth that you profess your faith and are saved. (NIV)
                 <br/>
                 <em>
                  If you’re wondering what to do next as a new Christian, check out these helpful suggestions:
                 </em>
                </p>
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  —
                 </strong>
                 Salvation is by grace, through faith. There’s nothing you did, or ever can do, to deserve it. It’s a free gift from God. All you have to do is receive it!
                 <br/>
                 <strong>
                  —
                 </strong>
                 Tell someone about your decision. It’s important that you tell someone to make it public, secure, and firm. Find a brother or sister in the Lord and tell him or her, “Hey, I made a decision to follow Jesus.” And do it today if you can. It’s a great way to seal the deal.
                 <br/>
                 <strong>
                  —
                 </strong>
                 Talk to God every day. You don’t have to use big fancy words. There are no right and wrong words. Just be yourself. Thank the Lord daily for your salvation. Pray for others in need. Seek his direction. Pray for the Lord to fill you daily with his Holy Spirit. There is no limit to prayer. You can pray with your eyes closed or open, while sitting or standing, kneeling or lying on your bed, anywhere, and anytime.
                </p>
                <p>
                 –Read the Bible everyday. God will speak to you through His Word! It is life giving and is our guide book in life!
                </p>
                <p>
                 –Get involved in a church. Being a part of a church not only helps you to grow spiritually but will assist you in developing into the person that God intended you to be. We were not made to do this life alone!
                </p>
                <p>
                 If you prayed this prayer and asked Jesus into your heart or even re-dedicated your life to Christ then we would love to hear from you! Please email info@mercygatechurch.com and let us know or you can call our church office at 281-576-5201 and ask to talk to one of our staff pastors! God BLESS YOU!
                </p>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>

             <h1 class="boc_heading al_left boc_animate_when_almost_visible boc_top-to-bottom" style="margin-bottom: 20px;margin-top: 0px;color: #282828;font-size: 28px;">
              <span>
               Meet
               <strong>
                Our Mercy Gate
               </strong>
               Staff!
              </span>
             </h1>
             <h4 class="boc_heading al_left boc_animate_when_almost_visible boc_fade-in" style="margin-bottom: 20px;margin-top: 0px;color: #939393;font-size: 20px;">
              <span>
               We have a blast serving Jesus, His people, and each other. We enjoy what we do and are honored to serve!
              </span>
             </h4>
             <div class="content_slides content_slides_arrowed has_dots" id="content_slides_3441">
              <div class="content_slide_item ">
               <div class="vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid vc_column-gap-10 vc_row-o-equal-height vc_row-flex">
                <div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-3">

             <h1 class="boc_heading center boc_subheading " style="margin-bottom: 20px;margin-top: 0px;color: #ededed;">
              <span>
               MercyGate Discipleship Track
              </span>
             </h1>
             <h1 class="boc_heading center " style="margin-bottom: 20px;margin-top: 0px;color: #ededed;">
              <span>
               What’s Next for You?
              </span>
             </h1>
             <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element #white text">
              <div class="wpb_wrapper">
               <h6>
               </h6>
               <p>
                At MercyGate, we believe that you can’t grow with God by staying where you are at. We should always be advancing and moving forward in order to live victoriously! Your next step might be to simply learn more about Jesus and decide to follow Him faithfully. Maybe your next step is to join a small group or find a place to serve, be baptized, or maybe you want to be a better leader or become more knowledgeable regarding the Bible. Whatever your next step is, we encourage you to take it. Remember that you are never alone…we are here to help you ever step of the way!
               </p>
               <p>
                We encourage every MercyGate attendee to be a part of Next Step Growth Track! These classes will help you grow spiritually and assist you in understanding the Bible and how to grow deeper in your relationship with Christ. We also will have some other classes to accent our Next Steps such as courses on living a life free of offenses, how to live a life with honor, developing a Kingdom mindset and more!
               </p>
               <p>
                Click on the button below to see the next dates, classes and sign up information for our Next Steps Growth Track!
               </p>

             <h1 class="boc_heading white text# center " style="margin-bottom: 20px;margin-top: 0px;color: #ffffff;font-size: 25;">
              <span>
               MercyGate Groups!
              </span>
             </h1>
             <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element ">
              <div class="wpb_wrapper">
               <p>
                <img alt="" class="alignleft wp-image-25857" data-attachment-id="25857" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"1503493192","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"1"}' data-image-title="MGC Groups single fold" data-large-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/MGC-Groups-single-fold.jpg?fit=840%2C1024" data-medium-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/MGC-Groups-single-fold.jpg?fit=246%2C300" data-orig-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/MGC-Groups-single-fold.jpg?fit=1807%2C2202" data-orig-size="1807,2202" data-permalink="http://www.mercygatechurch.com/welcome-home/mgc-groups-single-fold/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="609" sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" src="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/MGC-Groups-single-fold.jpg?resize=500%2C609" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/MGC-Groups-single-fold.jpg?resize=840%2C1024 840w, https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/MGC-Groups-single-fold.jpg?resize=246%2C300 246w, https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/MGC-Groups-single-fold.jpg?resize=768%2C936 768w" width="500"/>
               </p>
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="boc_spacing " style="height: 50px">
             </div>
             <div class="boc_spacing " style="height: 50px">
             </div>
             <div class="boc_spacing " style="height: 50px">
             </div>
             <div class="boc_spacing " style="height: 50px">
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6 vc_col-has-fill" id="#white text">
           <div class="vc_column-inner vc_custom_1516941519734">
            <div class="wpb_wrapper">
             <div class="boc_spacing " style="height: 50px">
             </div>
             <div class="boc_spacing " style="height: 50px">
             </div>
             <div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element vc_custom_1518465681138 #white text" id="h6">
              <div class="wpb_wrapper">
               <p>
                At MercyGate Church we have tons of ways that you can find community and connection and MercyGate Groups is one of them! We all know how important it is to connect on a smaller level at a larger church….to learn, to find friends and to grow in a way that you would never be able to on your own. So that is why you need to join one of our MercyGate Groups! We have groups that meet at homes, groups that go on couple date nights, groups that go out and serve our community and more! Some of our groups will meet weekly and some monthly so you have every opportunity to find something that is perfect just for YOU!
               </p>
               <p>
                <strong>
                 Home Groups
                </strong>
                meet together twice a month to have food, share some laughs and join together in a time of sharing God’s Word at a members house. The discussions are comfortable and encouraging and is a great place where friendships are formed. Click at the button below to see what Home Groups are available at this time.
               </p>
               <p>
                <strong>
                 Connect Groups
                </strong>
                meet at various times and are centered around interests and activities. These groups are held on golf courses, in restaurants, at the mall or during church times as a volunteer.
               </p>
               <p>
                <strong>
                 Serve Groups
                </strong>
                exist inside and outside of the church. They provide a way for you to use your talents to honor God. Here at MercyGate Church, we’ve have serve groups for coffee baristas, audio/visual, greeters and even emergency medical people!  YOUR talents can be used in our office, in the parking lot, on stage, or helping to keep the church beautiful. Outside of the church, we are always looking for people that are willing to serve others through various opportunities like driving, providing meals, or maybe just offering up a friendly visit or phone call. No matter how little that you feel you can give to serve, there is a way for you to change someone’s world through just one day in a serve group.
               </p>
               <p>
                There is a group just for you available so click on the MercyGate Groups button below!
               </p>
              </div>
             </div>
             <a class="button btn_huge btn_theme_color btn_rounded btn_gradient " href="http://www.mercygatechurch.com/2017/08/mercygate-home-groups/" target="_self">
              <span>
               MercyGate Groups
              </span>
             </a>
             <div class="boc_spacing " style="height: 50px">
             </div>

                <img alt="" class="wp-image-26381 alignleft" data-attachment-id="26381" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="1417539397" data-large-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1417539397-2.png?fit=725%2C254" data-medium-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1417539397-2.png?fit=300%2C105" data-orig-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1417539397-2.png?fit=725%2C254" data-orig-size="725,254" data-permalink="http://www.mercygatechurch.com/welcome-home/1417539397-3/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="183" sizes="(max-width: 523px) 100vw, 523px" src="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1417539397-2.png?resize=523%2C183" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1417539397-2.png?resize=300%2C105 300w, https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1417539397-2.png?w=725 725w" width="523"/>
                Mercy Gate Learning Center is a wonderful, loving, Christian environment that provides children with a strong academic and socio-emotional foundation and positive first school experience.  From six weeks to school age, all children at MGLC are given an opportunity to explore, experiment, and create in a safe and nurturing environment. We are now taking applications for our private Kindergarten class for the 2018-2019 school year!
               </p>

              <div class="acc_item">
               <h4 class="accordion">
                <span class="acc_control ">
                </span>
                <span class="acc_heading">
                 MercyGate Youth
                </span>
               </h4>
               <div class="accordion_content">
                <em>
                 <img alt="mgy-logo-16-1080-b" class="alignleft wp-image-25230 size-medium" data-attachment-id="25230" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="mgy-logo-16-1080-b" data-large-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/mgy-logo-16-1080-b.png?fit=1024%2C576" data-medium-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/mgy-logo-16-1080-b.png?fit=300%2C169" data-orig-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/mgy-logo-16-1080-b.png?fit=1920%2C1080" data-orig-size="1920,1080" data-permalink="http://www.mercygatechurch.com/welcome-home/mgy-logo-16-1080-b-2/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="169" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i0.wp.com/mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/mgy-logo-16-1080-b-300x169.png?resize=300%2C169" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/mgy-logo-16-1080-b.png?resize=300%2C169 300w, https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/mgy-logo-16-1080-b.png?resize=768%2C432 768w, https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/mgy-logo-16-1080-b.png?resize=1024%2C576 1024w" width="300"/>
                 Our MercyGate Youth Student Pastors Quinton &amp; Aubreana Carter desire to see students, who look, live and love like Jesus. We are all just ordinary people growing in relationship with an extraordinary God – and our students are no exception to this! MercyGate Youth isn’t just one more activity to add to their already full schedules, but rather is the place for junior high and senior high school students to connect relationally to one another and to discover the radical grace of God in a fresh and new way!
                </em>
                <br/>
                You are welcome here in this youth ministry! No matter who you are or what you’ve done. No matter your past or background; color, race, lifestyle, or appearance will NOT stop God’s love for you nor our love for you!
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  <em>
                   Fine Arts, Missions and Camp
                  </em>
                 </strong>
                 <br/>
                 Come join us for the opportunity to develop and deploy your gifts and talents for the glory of God through Fine Arts. We also know you can change the world, one heart at a time through missions. We go on several missions and evangelical outreaches, trips, and opportunities to show the love of Christ to others any way we can.
                </p>
                <p>
                </p>
                <p>
                 We look forward to having you at MercyGate Youth! Join us on Wednesday evenings at 7pm in the Youth Room! For more information or questions contact Pastor Quinton.
                 <a href="mailto:quinton@mercygatechurch.com">
                  quinton@mercygatechurch.com
                 </a>
                 . Check out the Events page on this website for updated youth activities!
                </p>
                <p>
                </p>
                <p>
                 Connect with us on social media:
                 <a href="https://www.facebook.com/MercyGateYouth/">
                  MercyGate Youth Facebook
                 </a>
                 <a href="https://www.instagram.com/mgy_youth/">
                  MercyGate Youth Instagram
                 </a>
                </p>
               </div>
              </div>

                <img alt="prayer" class="size-thumbnail wp-image-24946 alignright" data-attachment-id="24946" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="prayer" data-large-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/prayer.jpg?fit=275%2C183" data-medium-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/prayer.jpg?fit=275%2C183" data-orig-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/prayer.jpg?fit=275%2C183" data-orig-size="275,183" data-permalink="http://www.mercygatechurch.com/welcome-home/prayer/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="150" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" src="https://i1.wp.com/mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/prayer-150x150.jpg?resize=150%2C150" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/prayer.jpg?resize=150%2C150 150w, https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/prayer.jpg?resize=180%2C180 180w" width="150"/>
                Prayer is very important to MercyGate Church. We have intercessors, prayer partners, altar workers etc that cover our Pastors and church in prayer every single day and during all services. If you want to be a part of our prayer team or get information regarding regular scheduled meetings;  you can contact our Prayer Director Annette Bean at
                <a href="mailtoAnnette@mercygatechurch.com">
                 Annette@mercygatechurch.com
                </a>

              <div class="acc_item">
               <h4 class="accordion">
                <span class="acc_control ">
                </span>
                <span class="acc_heading">
                 Healing Rooms
                </span>
               </h4>
               <div class="accordion_content">
                <em>
                 <img alt="IMG_2077" class="size-thumbnail wp-image-25326 alignleft" data-attachment-id="25326" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"1"}' data-image-title="IMG_2077" data-large-file="https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/IMG_2077-1.jpg?fit=805%2C1024" data-medium-file="https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/IMG_2077-1.jpg?fit=236%2C300" data-orig-file="https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/IMG_2077-1.jpg?fit=4950%2C6300" data-orig-size="4950,6300" data-permalink="http://www.mercygatechurch.com/events/healing-rooms/img_2077-2/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="150" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" src="https://i2.wp.com/mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/IMG_2077-1-150x150.jpg?resize=150%2C150" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/IMG_2077-1.jpg?resize=150%2C150 150w, https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/IMG_2077-1.jpg?resize=180%2C180 180w, https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/IMG_2077-1.jpg?resize=300%2C300 300w, https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/IMG_2077-1.jpg?resize=600%2C600 600w, https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/IMG_2077-1.jpg?zoom=3&amp;resize=150%2C150 450w" width="150"/>
                 Healing Rooms is organized by our Pastor Holly Murray.
                </em>
                <div>
                 <b>
                  <u>
                   What is MercyGate Healing Rooms?
                  </u>
                 </b>
                </div>
                <div>
                 MercyGate Healing Rooms is an opportunity for the people of MercyGate Church and the community at large to receive prayer for physical healing. We host MGHR once per month on every 3rd Thursday of the month. If possible, please schedule your prayer time with us so we can best plan for you to be there.
                </div>
                <div>
                </div>
                <div>
                 At MercyGate Healing Rooms, from 7:00-7:30 p.m. we have a time of welcome, a short teaching about healing, and then some worship. We cultivate a calm, peaceful, loving atmosphere. When it is your turn for prayer, you are seated with a group consisting of 3 Healing Team Members. Once your prayer time has finished, you are welcomed to remain in the Sanctuary or you are free to leave and enjoy the rest of your evening.
                </div>
                <div>
                </div>
                <div>
                 <i>
                  *Please note that we are happy to pray for your child or teen at Healing Rooms, but there is no childcare available for additional children who attend at this time.
                 </i>
                </div>
                <div>
                </div>
                <div>
                 <b>
                  <u>
                   How do I Sign-up for MercyGate Healing Rooms?
                  </u>
                 </b>
                </div>
                <div>
                 We would be honored to pray with you and believe God for total healing in your body! If you are interested in participating in our next MGHR. Please click the link below to fill out the form online to sign-up:
                </div>
                <div>
                 <div>
                  <div>
                   <div>
                   </div>
                   <div>
                    <span style="color: #000000;">
                     <a dir="ltr" href="https://form.jotform.com/MercyGate/mercygate-healing-rooms-intake-form" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
                      https://form.jotform.com/Mercy
                     </a>
                     <a dir="ltr" href="https://form.jotform.com/MercyGate/mercygate-healing-rooms-intake-form" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
                      Gate/mercygate-healing-rooms-i
                     </a>
                     <a dir="ltr" href="https://form.jotform.com/MercyGate/mercygate-healing-rooms-intake-form" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
                      ntake-form
                     </a>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <div>
                   <span style="color: #000000;">
                   </span>
                  </div>
                  <div>
                   Prayer at MGHR occurs from 7:30-8:30 p.m. on a first come, first serve basis. Prayer times last approximately 10-15 minutes.
                   <span style="color: #000000;">
                    <i>
                     <br/>
                    </i>
                   </span>
                  </div>
                  <div>
                  </div>
                  <div>
                   <span style="color: #000000;">
                    <i>
                     *Please note that our Healing Rooms fill up in advance from time to time. As such, please be prepared to attend the following month’s Healing Room if the one you requested is already full. Thank you for your understanding!
                    </i>
                   </span>
                  </div>
                  <div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div>
                  For more information or any questions that you may have; please contact Pastor Holly Murray at Holly@mercygatechurch.com
                 </div>
                </div>
                <p>
                </p>
               </div>
              </div>

                </span>
                <span class="acc_heading">
                 Covered In Love
                </span>
               </h4>
               <div class="accordion_content">
                Cove
                <img alt="1026191_4013254386064_283457211_o" class="alignleft wp-image-25197 size-thumbnail" data-attachment-id="25197" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="1026191_4013254386064_283457211_o" data-large-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1026191_4013254386064_283457211_o-e1478579885493.jpg?fit=851%2C1024" data-medium-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1026191_4013254386064_283457211_o-e1478579885493.jpg?fit=249%2C300" data-orig-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1026191_4013254386064_283457211_o-e1478579885493.jpg?fit=1040%2C1251" data-orig-size="1040,1251" data-permalink="http://www.mercygatechurch.com/welcome-home/1026191_4013254386064_283457211_o/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="150" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px" src="https://i1.wp.com/mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1026191_4013254386064_283457211_o-e1478579885493-150x150.jpg?resize=150%2C150" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1026191_4013254386064_283457211_o-e1478579885493.jpg?resize=150%2C150 150w, https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1026191_4013254386064_283457211_o-e1478579885493.jpg?resize=180%2C180 180w, https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1026191_4013254386064_283457211_o-e1478579885493.jpg?resize=300%2C300 300w, https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1026191_4013254386064_283457211_o-e1478579885493.jpg?resize=600%2C600 600w, https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1026191_4013254386064_283457211_o-e1478579885493.jpg?zoom=3&amp;resize=150%2C150 450w" width="150"/>
                red in Love is a wonderful ministry through MercyGate Church! It’s founder and leader is Wendy Jackson and you can contact her via email through info@mercygatechurch.com  This ministry is a blanket ministry for the sick and hurting. Someone requests a blanket and lets the leader knows what is going on and then the group gets together and as they make the blanket they pray over the person and situation. Then they deliver or mail the blanket to the recipient with the prayer and scriptures to let them know that there are people praying for them and believing for them. This ministry has seen so many wonderful testimonies and is such a blessing to the community.
               </div>
              </div>

               <h4 class="accordion">
                <span class="acc_control ">
                </span>
                <span class="acc_heading">
                 MercyGate Kids
                </span>
               </h4>
               <div class="accordion_content">
                <img alt="" class="size-medium wp-image-26388 alignleft" data-attachment-id="26388" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="Logo_01_wTL" data-large-file="https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Logo_01_wTL.png?fit=900%2C600" data-medium-file="https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Logo_01_wTL.png?fit=300%2C200" data-orig-file="https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Logo_01_wTL.png?fit=900%2C600" data-orig-size="900,600" data-permalink="http://www.mercygatechurch.com/welcome-home/logo_01_wtl/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="200" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Logo_01_wTL.png?resize=300%2C200" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Logo_01_wTL.png?resize=300%2C200 300w, https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Logo_01_wTL.png?resize=768%2C512 768w, https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Logo_01_wTL.png?w=900 900w" width="300"/>
                Here at MercyGate Church your kids are a really big deal! Not only do we value their safety just as much as you do, but we also get the fun factor. While you’re in service, rest assured that your kids are receiving top-notch, age-appropriate care with a splash of mind-blowing experiences, rooted in the truth of God’s radical grace. Now that’s something worth getting excited about! We have kids services during any regularly scheduled adult service for your convenience.
                <p>
                 Children from all walks of life are accepted and loved at Mercygate Kids. We strive to make our campus a safe place for children physically, mentally, and spiritually. No matter what happens to your child throughout the week, MercyGate Kids is a stable, fun environment for them to experience Christ and to be exactly who God created them to be! Each week at MercyGate Kids, our goal is to help your child grow in their relationship with Christ, identify their gifts, and utilize their talents to further the Kingdom of Heaven.
                </p>
                <p>
                 Our moto is “Where Your Child Belongs”. I would say my biggest want out of our children’s ministry is not just the willingness to minister to all children but to have the capability to minister to all children including special needs. I want us to be able to effectively minister to children from all walks of life. No one is turned away.
                </p>
                <p>
                 MercyGate Kids exists to disciple children through the basics of biblical knowledge and the fundamentals of having a relationship with Jesus Christ; while giving parents the tools they need to continue that discipleship at home.
                </p>
                <p>
                 Click the link to get updated information &amp; current events:
                 <a href="http://www.mercygatechurch.com/2018/03/26389/">
                  Click HERE
                 </a>
                </p>
                <p>
                 Connect with MercyGate Kids via FB here:
                 <a href="https://www.facebook.com/MercyGateKids/">
                  MercyGate Kids Facebook
                 </a>
                </p>
               </div>

              <div class="acc_item">
               <h4 class="accordion">
                <span class="acc_control ">
                </span>
                <span class="acc_heading">
                 Freedom Ministry
                </span>
               </h4>
               <div class="accordion_content">
                <img class="wp-image-24954 size-full alignleft" data-attachment-id="24954" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="freedom-ministries" data-large-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/freedom-ministries.jpg?fit=356%2C142" data-medium-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/freedom-ministries.jpg?fit=300%2C120" data-orig-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/freedom-ministries.jpg?fit=356%2C142" data-orig-size="356,142" data-permalink="http://www.mercygatechurch.com/welcome-home/freedom-ministries/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="142" sizes="(max-width: 356px) 100vw, 356px" src="https://i1.wp.com/mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/freedom-ministries.jpg?resize=356%2C142" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/freedom-ministries.jpg?w=356 356w, https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/freedom-ministries.jpg?resize=300%2C120 300w" width="356"/>
                Pastor Holly Murray is over our Freedom ministries here at MercyGate Church.
                <div>
                 <b>
                  <u>
                   What is MercyGate
                   <span class="m_2756136130394806568gmail-il">
                    Freedom
                   </span>
                   Ministries?
                  </u>
                 </b>
                </div>
                <div>
                 <div>
                  We believe that
                  <span class="m_2756136130394806568gmail-il">
                   freedom
                  </span>
                  is not the absence of something, but the presence of someone– namely, Jesus Christ. We teach people how to engage the presence of God for inner healing, discipleship and empowerment to grow in your relationship with Christ.
                 </div>
                 <div>
                 </div>
                 <div>
                 </div>
                 <div>
                  <b>
                   <u>
                    What is an individual
                    <span class="m_2756136130394806568gmail-il">
                     Freedom
                    </span>
                    Session?
                   </u>
                  </b>
                 </div>
                 <div>
                  <span class="m_2756136130394806568gmail-il">
                   Freedom
                  </span>
                  sessions consist of the person meeting with a member of the
                  <span class="m_2756136130394806568gmail-il">
                   Freedom
                  </span>
                  Team. We typically have a session intercessor present whose job is to quietly pray throughout the session. We teach people how to personally hear the voice of God in their lives empowering them to learn about their identity in Christ as well as equipping them with practical tools such as learning about the gift of forgiveness, how to renew the mind, and through prayerfully healing life hurts.
                 </div>
                 <div>
                 </div>
                 <div>
                  <span class="m_2756136130394806568gmail-il">
                   Freedom
                  </span>
                  Ministries is not a counseling ministry. Rather, it is a prayer-based ministry. Referrals for professional Christian counsel
                  <wbr>
                  </wbr>
                  ing are available upon request.
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div>
                </div>
                <div>
                 <b>
                  <u>
                   How May I Schedule a
                   <span class="m_2756136130394806568gmail-il">
                    Freedom
                   </span>
                   Session?
                  </u>
                 </b>
                </div>
                <div>
                 To schedule a Freedom Session with a member of our Freedom Ministries Team, please contact Pastor Holly Murray at
                 <a href="mailto:holly@mercygatechurch.com" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
                  holly@mercygatechurch.com
                 </a>
                 .
                </div>
                <div>
                </div>
                <div>
                 A huge part of the
                 <span class="m_2756136130394806568gmail-il">
                  Freedom
                 </span>
                 Ministries journey is learning a new way of thinking especially about God and ourselves. The first step in that process is to take the
                 <span class="m_2756136130394806568gmail-il">
                  Freedom
                 </span>
                 Basics classes. We are not presently offering the
                 <span class="m_2756136130394806568gmail-il">
                  Freedom
                 </span>
                 Basics classes at MercyGate Church, but we have them available for you to view online through Gateway Church in Southlake, Texas. Prior to scheduling a session, we ask you to listen to
                 <span class="m_2756136130394806568gmail-il">
                  Freedom
                 </span>
                 Basics 101-104 which can be found at the link below:
                </div>
                <div>
                </div>
                <div>
                 <a href="https://gatewaypeople.com/ministries/freedom/events/freedom-basics" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
                  https://gatewaypeople.com/
                  <wbr>
                  </wbr>
                  ministries/
                  <span class="m_2756136130394806568gmail-il">
                   freedom
                  </span>
                  /events/
                  <span class="m_2756136130394806568gmail-il">
                   free
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   dom
                  </span>
                  -basics
                 </a>
                </div>
                <p>
                </p>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="acc_item">
               <h4 class="accordion">
                <span class="acc_control ">
                </span>
                <span class="acc_heading">
                 MercyGate Groups
                </span>
               </h4>
               <div class="accordion_content">
                <h4>
                 <strong>
                  <img alt="" class="size-medium wp-image-26265 alignleft" data-attachment-id="26265" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"1"}' data-image-title="Groupd Sign up here 24×36 back" data-large-file="https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/Groupd-Sign-up-here-24x36-back-1.jpg?fit=683%2C1024" data-medium-file="https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/Groupd-Sign-up-here-24x36-back-1.jpg?fit=200%2C300" data-orig-file="https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/Groupd-Sign-up-here-24x36-back-1.jpg?fit=3600%2C5400" data-orig-size="3600,5400" data-permalink="http://www.mercygatechurch.com/events/mercygate-groups-2/groupd-sign-up-here-24x36-back-2/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="300" sizes="(max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px" src="https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/Groupd-Sign-up-here-24x36-back-1.jpg?resize=200%2C300" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/Groupd-Sign-up-here-24x36-back-1.jpg?resize=200%2C300 200w, https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/Groupd-Sign-up-here-24x36-back-1.jpg?resize=768%2C1152 768w, https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/Groupd-Sign-up-here-24x36-back-1.jpg?resize=683%2C1024 683w, https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/Groupd-Sign-up-here-24x36-back-1.jpg?w=2400 2400w, https://i0.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/Groupd-Sign-up-here-24x36-back-1.jpg?w=3600 3600w" width="200"/>
                 </strong>
                </h4>
                <p>
                 At MercyGate Church we have tons of ways that you can find community and connection and MercyGate Groups is one of them! We all know how important it is to connect on a smaller level at a larger church….to learn, to find friends and to grow in a way that you would never be able to on your own. So that is why you need to join one of our MercyGate Groups! We have groups that meet at homes, groups that go on couple date nights, groups that go out and serve our community and more! Some of our groups will meet weekly and some monthly so you have every opportunity to find something that is perfect just for YOU!
                </p>
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  Home Groups
                 </strong>
                 meet together twice a month to have food, share some laughs and join together in a time of sharing God’s Word at a members house. The discussions are comfortable and encouraging and is a great place where friendships are formed. Click on the button below to see what Home Groups are available at this time.
                </p>
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  Connect Groups
                 </strong>
                 meet at various times and are centered around interests and activities. These groups are held on golf courses, in restaurants, at the mall or on a date night with other couples. They are held weekly or monthly as announced. You want to make sure that you sign up for one of these fun and wonderful groups! Click on the link below to see what Connect Groups are available.
                </p>
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  Serve Groups
                 </strong>
                 exist inside and outside of the church. They provide a way for you to use your talents to honor God. Here at MercyGate Church, we’ve have serve groups for coffee baristas, audio/visual, greeters and even emergency medical people!  YOUR talents can be used in our office, in the parking lot, on stage, or helping to keep the church beautiful. Outside of the church, we are always looking for people that are willing to serve others through various opportunities like driving, providing meals, or maybe just offering up a friendly visit or phone call. No matter how little that you feel you can give to serve, there is a way for you to change someone’s world through just one day in a serve group.
                </p>
                <p>
                 There is a group just for YOU so click on the the link:
                 <a href="http://www.mercygatechurch.com/2017/08/mercygate-groups/">
                  MercyGate Groups
                 </a>
                </p>
                <p>
                </p>
               </div>
              </div>

              <div class="acc_item">
               <h4 class="accordion">
                <span class="acc_control ">
                </span>
                <span class="acc_heading">
                 15 in 5 Devotional
                </span>
               </h4>
               <div class="accordion_content">
                <strong>
                 <img alt="1604730_647742558669892_3455682075588789751_n" class="alignleft wp-image-25007 size-medium" data-attachment-id="25007" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="1604730_647742558669892_3455682075588789751_n" data-large-file="https://i1.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1604730_647742558669892_3455682075588789751_n.jpg?fit=960%2C447" data-medium-file="https://i1.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1604730_647742558669892_3455682075588789751_n.jpg?fit=300%2C140" data-orig-file="https://i1.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1604730_647742558669892_3455682075588789751_n.jpg?fit=960%2C447" data-orig-size="960,447" data-permalink="http://www.mercygatechurch.com/welcome-home/1604730_647742558669892_3455682075588789751_n/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="140" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i0.wp.com/mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1604730_647742558669892_3455682075588789751_n-300x140.jpg?resize=300%2C140" srcset="https://i1.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1604730_647742558669892_3455682075588789751_n.jpg?resize=300%2C140 300w, https://i1.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1604730_647742558669892_3455682075588789751_n.jpg?resize=768%2C358 768w, https://i1.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/1604730_647742558669892_3455682075588789751_n.jpg?w=960 960w" width="300"/>
                 15 and 5 Daily Devotionals!
                </strong>
                <br/>
                “Fifteen in Five” is MercyGate Church’s daily devotional that is based primarily on our Sunday morning messages. We ask you to take fifteen minutes out of your day and reflect on the devotion, five days a week. Along with a devotion, there will be prayer points to guide you as you reflect on the message.
                <br/>
                <strong>
                 You can access these devotions 3 different ways:
                </strong>
                <br/>
                #1. Via email: Signup for 15 in 5 by emailing:
                <a href="info@mercygatechurch.com">
                 info@mercygatechurch.com
                </a>
                and make sure you put “15 in 5 sign up” in the subject line!
                <br/>
                #2. The “15 in 5” devotion you can read via our church app. Get Our Church App here:
                <a href="http://subsplash.com/mercygatechurch">
                 MercyGate Church App
                </a>
                <br/>
                #3. Or you can click on the blog link below and follow the blog to get the updates.
                <br/>
                Blog Link to 15 in 5 devotional:
                <a href="http://15in5mercygatechurchdevotionals.blogspot.com">
                 15 in 5 MercyGate Devotional
                </a>
               </div>
              </div>

               <h4 class="accordion">

                <span class="acc_heading">
                 Innovate Business Leaders
                </span>
               </h4>
               <div class="accordion_content">
                <img alt="innovate1" class="alignnone wp-image-25236 size-medium" data-attachment-id="25236" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="innovate1" data-large-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Innovate1.jpg?fit=1024%2C730" data-medium-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Innovate1.jpg?fit=300%2C214" data-orig-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Innovate1.jpg?fit=3344%2C2383" data-orig-size="3344,2383" data-permalink="http://www.mercygatechurch.com/welcome-home/innovate1/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="214" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i2.wp.com/mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Innovate1-300x214.jpg?resize=300%2C214" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Innovate1.jpg?resize=300%2C214 300w, https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Innovate1.jpg?resize=768%2C547 768w, https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Innovate1.jpg?resize=1024%2C730 1024w, https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Innovate1.jpg?w=2400 2400w" width="300"/>
                <img alt="innovate2" class="wp-image-25237 size-medium alignnone" data-attachment-id="25237" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="innovate2" data-large-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Innovate2.jpg?fit=1024%2C730" data-medium-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Innovate2.jpg?fit=300%2C214" data-orig-file="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Innovate2.jpg?fit=3344%2C2383" data-orig-size="3344,2383" data-permalink="http://www.mercygatechurch.com/welcome-home/innovate2/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="214" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i1.wp.com/mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Innovate2-300x214.jpg?resize=300%2C214" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Innovate2.jpg?resize=300%2C214 300w, https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Innovate2.jpg?resize=768%2C547 768w, https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Innovate2.jpg?resize=1024%2C730 1024w, https://i2.wp.com/www.mercygatechurch.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Innovate2.jpg?w=2400 2400w" width="300"/>
                <p>
                 MercyGate Innovate is a leadership group for business owners. It meets on the 4th Wednesday of every month from 7:30am to 8:30am. Anyone is welcome to join us for our breakfast! Pastor Don uses biblical business principles to teach Kingdom-minded leaders to be successful and unlock their potential. This group is a great opportunity to network with others to celebrate with you as well as assist you when answers are needed. If you are wanting more information email
                 <a href="mailto:Innovate@mercygatechurch.com">
                  Innovate@mercygatechurch.com
                 </a>
                 or check out the Events page on this website for the next Innovate Leadership Breakfast!
                 <a href="http://mercygatechurch.com/events/">
                  MercyGate Events
                 </a>
                </p>
